<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ли́ш(ний)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">líš(nij)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ек</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ek</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лишек.html>ли́шек</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">líšek</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лишек.html>ли́шка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лишек.html>ли́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лишек.html>ли́шков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> excess, surplus</li></ol>

***лишение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лишение.html>лише́ние</a> (6479)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лишить.html>лиши́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lišítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лишение.html>лише́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lišénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лишение.html>лише́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лишение.html>лише́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лишение.html>лише́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>deprivation</li>
<li>(usually plural) privations, hardship</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ше́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>е</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 7a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> словообразования: лишенье.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-лиш-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ениj</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-е</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>шён<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p>Страдательное <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прошедший.html>проше́дшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a/b(2).

***лишить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лишить.html>лиши́ть</a> (4586)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lišiti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*leykʷ-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lend</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">loan</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лишить.html>лиши́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lišítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лишать.html>лиша́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to deprive, to rob, to bereave
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>они́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишенный.html>лишены́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>самого</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:корённый.html>коренно́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>права</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oní <b>lišený</b> samovo korennóvo prava</i> ― <span class="e-translation">they are <b>deprived</b> of the most fundamental rights</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to devest, to forjudge, to dispossess
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишить.html>лиши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>прав</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišítʹ</b> prav</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to deprive / rob (smb.) of his rights</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишить.html>лиши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:наследство.html>насле́дства</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišítʹ</b> naslédstva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to disinherit</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишить.html>лиши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жи́зни</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišítʹ</b> sebjá žízni</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take one's life</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишить.html>лиши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>пра́ва</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>го́лоса</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišítʹ</b> práva gólosa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to disfranchise</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишить.html>лиши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:воинский.html>во́инских</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:звание.html>зва́ний</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišítʹ</b> vóinskix zvánij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to reduce to the ranks</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишить.html>лиши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́ва</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišítʹ</b> slóva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to deny (smb.) the right to speak</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишить.html>лиши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:парламентский.html>парла́ментского</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мандат.html>манда́та</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišítʹ</b> parlámentskovo mandáta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to unseat</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишить.html>лиши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:удовольствие.html>удово́льствия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišítʹ</b> sebjá udovólʹstvija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to deprive oneself</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишить.html>лиши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:духовный.html>духо́вного</a> са́на</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišítʹ</b> duxóvnovo sána</i> ― <span class="e-translation">defrock, unfrock</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишить.html>лиши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:гражданский.html>гражда́нских</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>прав</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišítʹ</b> graždánskix prav</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to disfranchise</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишить.html>лиши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:родительский.html>роди́тельских</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>прав</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišítʹ</b> rodítelʹskix prav</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to deprive of parental rights</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

***лишь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лишь.html>лишь</a> (199)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">лише</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">liše</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, originally comparative form of <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">лихъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lixŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bad</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">лише́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lyšé</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лишь.html>лишь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lišʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>only, merely, just
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишь.html>лишь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišʹ</b> by</i> ― <span class="e-translation">if only</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>as soon as
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишь.html>лишь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišʹ</b> tólʹko</i> ― <span class="e-translation">no sooner ... than</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">tólʹko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всего́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vsevó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:единственный.html>еди́нственно</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jedínstvenno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исключительно.html>исключи́тельно</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">isključítelʹno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kak tólʹko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:едва.html>едва́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jedvá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<h4><span id=".D0.A1.D0.B8.D0.BD.D0.BE.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.BC.D1.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Синонимы"><a href = vnd.unilang:синоним.html>Сино́нимы</a></span></h4>

***лов.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лов.html>лов</a> (22540)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lovъ</i>, cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">lov</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лов.html>лов</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lov</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лов.html>ло́ва</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лов.html>ло́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лов.html>ло́вов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>catching, hunting</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лов.html>лов</a></b>

***ловить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ловить.html>лови́ть</a> (1832)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lovìti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to (try to) catch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловить.html>лови́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lovítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поймать.html>пойма́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изловить.html>излови́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to catch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ловить.html>лови́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыба.html>ры́бу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lovítʹ</b> rýbu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to catch fish</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-лов-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ловкий.html>ло́вкий</a> (5573)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lovъkъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловкий.html>ло́вкий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lóvkij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:ловчий.html>ловче́е</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:ловчий.html>ловче́й</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ло́вче</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>adroit, dexterous, deft</li>
<li>cunning, smart, crafty, never at a loss</li>
<li>comfortable</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ловкость.html>ло́вкость</a> (9095)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловкий.html>ло́вкий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lóvkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловкость.html>ло́вкость</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lóvkostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловкость.html>ло́вкости</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловкость.html>ло́вкости</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловкость.html>ло́вкостей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>agility, adroitness, dexterity, deftness

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<h4><span id=".D0.A1.D0.B8.D0.BD.D0.BE.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.BC.D1.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Синонимы"><a href = vnd.unilang:синоним.html>Сино́нимы</a></span></h4>
<ol><li>частичн.: проворность, <a href = vnd.unilang:сноровка.html>сноро́вка</a>, умелость</li>

***ловчий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ловчий.html>ло́вчий</a> (14925)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловить.html>лови́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lovítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-чий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-čij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловчий.html>ло́вчий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lóvčij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>hunting
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ловчий.html>ло́вчие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:птица.html>пти́цы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lóvčije</b> ptícy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">hunting birds</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>serving as a snare/trap
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ловчий.html>ло́вчий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ров.html>ров</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lóvčij</b> rov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">trap</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловить.html>лови́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">lovítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловля.html>ло́вля</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">lóvlja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловец.html>лове́ц</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">lovéc</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловчий.html>ло́вчий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lóvčij</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловчий.html>ло́вчего</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловчий.html>ло́вчие</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловчий.html>ло́вчих</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ловить.html>ловя́щий</a> (1832)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***логово.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:логово.html>ло́гово</a> (10832)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:логово.html>ло́гово</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lógovo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:логово.html>ло́гова</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:логово.html>ло́гова</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:логово.html>ло́гов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>den, lair <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">home of certain animals, also figurative</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:логово.html>ло́гово</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:враг.html>врага́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lógovo</b> vragá</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>den</b> of the enemy</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>ло́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>го<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:иметь.html>Име́ет</a> омоформу <i><a href = vnd.unilang:логово.html>логов</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сущий.html>сущ</a>. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:лог.html>лог</a></i>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-лог-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ов</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-о</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лодка.html>ло́дка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lódka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лодочник.html>ло́дочник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lódočnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лодочник.html>ло́дочника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лодочник.html>ло́дочники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лодочник.html>ло́дочников</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ло́дочница</b>)
